[[H4714|But the Egyptians]] [[H120|are men,]] [[H3808|not]] [[H410|God;]] [[H5483|their horses]] [[H1320|are flesh,]] [[H3808|not]] [[H7307|spirit.]] [[H3068|When the LORD]] [[H5186|stretches out]] [[H3027|His hand,]] [[H5826|the helper]] [[H3782|will stumble]] [[H5826|and the one he helps]] [[H5307|will fall;]] [[H3605|both]] [[H3615|will perish]] [[H3162|together.]] ^3103

[[H3588|For]] [[H3541|this is what]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H559|has said]] [[H413|to me:]] [[H834|“Like]] [[H738|a lion]] [[H1897|roaring]] [[H3715|or a young lion]] [[H5921|over]] [[H2964|its prey—]] [[H834|and though]] [[H4393|a band]] [[H7462|of shepherds]] [[H7121|is called out]] [[H5921|against it,]] [[H3808|it is not]] [[H2865|terrified]] [[H6963|by their shouting]] [[H6031|or subdued]] [[H1995|by their clamor—]] [[H3651|so]] [[H3068|the LORD]] [[H6635|of Hosts]] [[H3381|will come down]] [[H6633|to do battle]] [[H5921|on]] [[H2022|Mount]] [[H6726|Zion]] ⟨and⟩ [[H5921|]] [[H1389|its heights.]] ^3104

[[H3808|No]] [[H738|lion]] [[H1961|will be]] [[H8033|there,]] [[H1077|and no]] [[H6530|vicious]] [[H2416|beast]] [[H5927|will go up on it.]] [[H3808|Such will not]] [[H4672|be found]] [[H8033|there,]] [[H1350|but the redeemed]] [[H1980|will walk upon it,]] ^3509

[[H7760|I will establish]] [[H226|a sign among them,]] [[H7971|and I will send]] [[H6412|survivors]] [[H1992|from among them]] [[H8659|to Tarshish,]] [[H6322|Put,]] [[H3865|and Lud]] [[H4900|the archers,]] ⟨to⟩ [[H8422|Tubal,]] [[H3120|Javan,]] [[H339|and the islands]] [[H7350|far away,]] ⟨and⟩ [[H413|to]] [[H1471|the nations]] [[H834|who]] [[H3808|have not]] [[H8085|heard]] [[H8088|of My fame]] [[H7200|or seen]] [[H3519|My glory.]] [[H5046|So they will proclaim]] [[H3519|My glory]] [[H1471|among the nations.]] ^6619

[[H935|And they will bring]] [[H3605|all]] [[H251|your brothers]] [[H3605|from all]] [[H1471|the nations]] [[H4503|as a gift]] [[H3068|to the LORD]] [[H5483|on horses]] [[H7393|and chariots]] [[H6632|and wagons,]] [[H6505|on mules]] [[H3753|and camels,]] [[H5921|to]] [[H6944|My holy]] [[H2022|mountain]] [[H3389|Jerusalem,”]] [[H559|says]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H834|“just as]] [[H1121|the Israelites]] [[H935|bring]] [[H4503|an offering]] [[H2889|in a clean]] [[H3627|vessel]] [[H1004|to the house]] [[H3068|of the LORD.]] ^6620

[[H1571|And I will]] [[H3947|select]] [[H1992|some of them]] [[H3548|as priests]] [[H3881|and Levites,”]] [[H559|says]] [[H3068|the LORD.]] ^6621

[[H3588|“For]] [[H834|just as]] [[H2319|the new]] [[H8064|heavens]] [[H2319|and the new]] [[H776|earth,]] [[H834|which]] [[H589|I]] [[H6213|will make,]] [[H5975|will endure]] [[H6440|before Me,”]] [[H5002|declares]] [[H3068|the LORD,]] [[H3651|“so]] [[H2233|your descendants]] [[H8034|and your name]] [[H5975|will endure.]] ^6622

[[H1767|From]] [[H2320|one New Moon]] [[H2320|to another]] [[H1767|and from]] [[H7676|one Sabbath]] [[H7676|to another,]] [[H3605|all]] [[H1320|mankind]] [[H935|will come]] [[H7812|to worship]] [[H6440|before Me,”]] [[H559|says]] [[H3068|the LORD.]] ^6623

[[H3318|“As they go forth,]] [[H7200|they will see]] [[H6297|the corpses]] [[H376|of the men]] [[H6586|who have rebelled against Me;]] [[H3588|for]] [[H8438|their worm]] [[H3808|will never]] [[H4191|die,]] [[H784|their fire]] [[H3808|will never]] [[H3518|be quenched,]] [[H1961|and they will be]] [[H1860|a horror]] [[H3605|to all]] [[H1320|mankind.”]] ^6624
